5a3(1): tu rgyu gcer bu cig dang 'jal ba dang / bdag la tshig rtsub mo dag mchi'o zhes rgyas par gsol to// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das 'dzum pa mdzad nas/

5a8(1): de yid shin tu mnyam zhing gzhi bai nurar+ya las byas pa/ gser btsems thig le'ur bres pa/ rin po che sna bdun gyi shing skyes pa/ shing de dag kyang ma

5b3(1): su gang ba/ rdzing gi gzhin pas kyang gser gi bye mas brdal ba/ rdzing gings bzhin gsung dam pa ldan pa'i me tog pad+ma dang / put+ta d+ha rI ka dang / pa rI/ 
5b4(1): ka dang / de ma yin pa'i me tog sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po shing rta'i phang lo tsam gyis chu'i stengs su khebs pa/ chu'i nang
5b5(1): du bya rnam pa sna tshogs kyang shin tu yid du 'ong ba'i sgra snyan pa 'byin no// rdzing de'i nang na rin po che sna bdun las byas pa'i gru yod do// de nas sems can mang
5b6(1): po 'dod dgur rtse zhing longs spyod do// rin po che'i shing de dag bri bar bar na/ seng ge'i khri mtho khyad kyi tshad gcig pa bshams nas/ rin po che sna bdun
5b7(1): gyis brgyan te/ lha rdzas kyi na bza' khri'i steng du/ rim par bting ba lha rdzas kyi spos kyi dri 'thul ba/ lha rdzas kyi me tog gis chal par bkram pa'o khrings/ 
5b8(1): de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i rgyal po skyil gung du bcas shing bzhugs pa las/ byang chub sems dpa' chad med pa bye ba brgya stong snyed mdun du bdar de thal
